   <script>
    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
       function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
       gtag('js', new Date());
       gtag('config', 'UA-334226-27');
 
       
       /**
        * Global error handler to track errors with gtag
        */
       function listener() {
          var data = {};
          var preventNativeHandler = false;
          var event;
 
          // For historical reasons we receive different arguments depending on
          // the error's origin and handler type.
          if (arguments[0] instanceof ErrorEvent) {
             // Modern style error, received an ErrorEvent object with all data.
             event = arguments[0];
             data.message = event.message;
             data.source = event.filename;
             data.lineno = event.lineno;
             data.colno = event.colno;
             preventNativeHandler = true;
          } else if (arguments[0] instanceof Event) {
             // Error was on an element and doesn't provide error information.
             event = arguments[0];
             data.message = 'Unhandled error on ' + event.srcElement.nodeName.toLowerCase() + ' element';
             preventNativeHandler = false;
          } else {
             // Older style error handling, received a list of individual arguments.
             data.message = arguments[0] || 'unknown';
             data.source = arguments[1] || 'unknown';
             data.lineno = arguments[2] || '0';
             data.colno = arguments[3] || '0';
             preventNativeHandler = true;
          }
 
          if (typeof window.gtag === 'function') {
             gtag('event', 'exception', {
                'description': data.message + (data.source ? ' in ' + data.source + ':' + data.lineno + ',' + data.colno : ''),
                'fatal': false
             });
          }
 
          return preventNativeHandler;
       }
 
       window.addEventListener('error', listener, true);
   </script>

      <section class="block block1">
       <h2>
        About Gear4music.com
       </h2>
       <p>
        Launched in 2003 and now with over 1.3 million registered customers, Gear4music.com is a leading retailer of musical instruments and music equipment. You can buy music gear from orchestral instruments to rock 'n' roll, including guitars, drum kits, digital pianos, saxophones and cellos, plus leading recording and studio equipment.
       </p>
       <p>
        From starter guitars to pro microphones and amps, the Gear4music.com online music shop has a huge range of music equipment available. Whether you're looking for a violin, keyboard, electronic drum kit or PA system, we can help.
       </p>
       <p>
        We've got some of the biggest brands in stock, including Yamaha, Roland, Casio, Fender, Ibanez, Alesis, Behringer &amp; Gibson, as well as our own great value Gear4music music product range.
       </p>
       <p>
        To receive excellent service and a great price on your next musical instrument purchase, try us now!
       </p>
      </section>
